1) PROJECT IDENTIFICATION
1.1) Name QualisBrasil
1.2) Creator Sandro Rautenberg
1.3) Homepage http://lodunicentro.aksw.org/
1.5) Purpose(s) Offering Qualis Periodical Index according to the principles Linked Open Data
1.6) Description QualisBrasil is part of http://lod.unicentro.br endpoint. It aims to aid researchers to collect Linked Open Data about Qualis Index in bibliometrics or scientometrics studies. Available data: Periodical ISSN, Periodical Name, Knowledge Field, Qualis Index, and Year.
2) PLANNING WORKFLOW
Name Maintain QualisBrasil
What should be done Workflow applied to create linked dataset of Qualis Periodicals Index (all years), in an automatized way.
Precondition 1. Availability of the data (sql dump or what is there) 2. Running system with installed Ubuntu and all necessary tools (i.e. Sparqlify, Virtuoso, virt-load and all the scripts)
Postcondition QualisBrasil Graph is created and maintained.
Step(s)
step (1) ldwStep_01_qualisBrasil_from_legacy_system
task classification [Extract data from legacy systems/databases]
output dataset(s) name : evaluations.csv
format : CSV Format
location : tests/Graphs/QualisBrasil/csv/
license : No license defined
tool name: MySQL
location: /usr/share/mysql
what should be done here will be described what should be done in the PlanningStep - Extracting QualisBrasil from Legacy System
command real/QualisBrasilProject/bin/extractingFromLegacySystem.sh
step (2) ldwStep_02_qualisBrasil_converting_data_with_sparqlify
task classification [Convert data to compatible formats in Linked Data Applications]
input dataset(s) name : evaluations.csv
format : CSV Format
location : tests/Graphs/QualisBrasil/csv/
license : No license defined
output dataset(s) name : evolutions.nt
format : N-triples Format
location : tests/Graphs/QualisBrasil/nt/
license : Creative Commons public domain waiver
tool name: Sparqlify
location: /usr/share/lib/sparqlify/
what should be done What should be done to Extracting QualisBrasil applying SPARQLIFY is described here
command real/QualisBrasilProject/bin/applyingSparqlify.sh
tool configuration name : mappingQualis.sml
location : tests/QualisBrasilProject/Mappings/
step (3) ldwStep_03_qualisBrasil_storing_converted_data
task classification [Storage the graph]
input dataset(s) name : QualisBrasil.nt
format : N-triples Format
location : tests/Graphs/QualisBrasil/
license : Creative Commons public domain waiver
output dataset(s) name : Qualis Brasil Graph
format : RDF/XML Format
location : space.sina.aksw.org/sparql
license : Creative Commons public domain waiver
what should be done In this step the file QualisBrasil.nt is uploaded to Virtuoso by executing the command based on the toolConfiguration file.
command real/commons/savingIntoVirtuoso.sh real/Graphs/QualisBrasil/QualisBrasil.nt http://lod.unicentro.br/QualisBrasil/
step (4) ldwStep_04_qualisBrasil_interlinking_data_with_LIMES
task classification [Interlinking task test]

format : N-triples Format
location : dbpedia.org/sparql
license : Creative Commons public domain waiver

name : Qualis Brasil Graph

format : N-triples Format
